### [169] [Age of Incorrect Information for Generic Discrete-Time Markov Sources](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28369)
*Konstantinos Bountrogiannis,Anthony Ephremides,Panagiotis Tsakalides,George Tzagkarakis*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 该研究针对采用HARQ协议的嘈杂通信系统，提出了一种分析年龄错误信息(AoII)的框架，通过约束马尔可夫决策过程(CMDP)建模优化问题，开发了多阈值和单阈值策略，使用相对值迭代和二分搜索算法求解，在传输率约束下显著优于周期调度策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实时监控系统中信息新鲜度至关重要，但在HARQ协议和传输率约束下的噪声环境中，如何优化AoII缺乏系统分析框架，需要设计高效策略来平衡信息准确性和资源消耗。

Method: 建立离散时间马尔可夫源的CMDP模型，证明最优策略是两种平稳策略的随机混合；提出依赖源头、接收器和包计数的多阈值策略类，利用阈值结构推导AoII和传输率的闭式表达式；采用相对值迭代配合二分搜索满足率约束。

Result: 数值实验表明，多阈值策略与全局最优策略性能相当，单阈值策略通过牺牲最优性实现更低计算复杂度，两者均显著优于周期性调度策略。

Conclusion: 该框架为HARQ系统下的AoII优化提供了有效解决方案，多阈值策略接近最优性能，单阈值策略为计算资源有限场景提供实用方案，实现了性能与复杂度的平衡。

Abstract: This work introduces a framework for analyzing the Age of Incorrect Information (AoII) in a real-time monitoring system with a generic discrete-time Markov source. We study a noisy communication system employing a hybrid automatic repeat request (HARQ) protocol, subject to a transmission rate constraint. The optimization problem is formulated as a constrained Markov decision process (CMDP), and it is shown that there exists an optimal policy that is a randomized mixture of two stationary policies. To overcome the intractability of computing the optimal stationary policies, we develop a multiple-threshold policy class where thresholds depend on the source, the receiver, and the packet count. By establishing a Markov renewal structure induced by threshold policies, we derive closed-form expressions for the long-term average AoII and transmission rate. The proposed policy is constructed via a relative value iteration algorithm that leverages the threshold structure to skip computations, combined with a bisection search to satisfy the rate constraint. To accommodate scenarios requiring lower computational complexity, we adapt the same technique to produce a simpler single-threshold policy that trades optimality for efficiency. Numerical experiments exhibit that both thresholdbased policies outperform periodic scheduling, with the multiplethreshold approach matching the performance of the globally optimal policy.

</details>


### [170] [Joint Detection and Identification for Scalable Control of Nanorobot Swarms under Harsh Communication Constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28412)
*Wafa Labidi,Holger Boche,Christian Deppe,Marc Geitz*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 联合检测与识别框架通过设备本地判断广播信号相关性，实现隐式寻址和子集激活，无需单独通信，适用于资源受限的大规模设备协调控制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 微纳尺度等资源受限设备在生物医学应用中面临能量、尺寸和通信能力严重限制的挑战，传统通信范式难以实现大规模设备的精确协调控制，特别是在靶向药物递送等需要空间选择性激活的场景中。

Method: 提出联合检测与识别框架，将通信范式从可靠消息传输转向控制导向，让设备本地判断广播信号是否相关，实现隐式寻址；结合感知功能形成检测、通信和执行的闭环系统；分析传感分辨率、通信约束与系统动态的相互作用。

Result: 识别表现出良好的渐近缩放特性，但实际实现受有限块长效应、噪声和延迟的支配；该框架通过提供可扩展子集选择的控制层抽象，补充现有物理层通信方法。

Conclusion: JDAI将识别理论原理与系统级设计相结合，为控制大规模、资源受限环境提供了一种有效的框架，特别适合靶向纳米机器人治疗等应用场景。

Abstract: The coordination of large populations of highly constrained devices, such as micro- and nanoscale agents in biomedical applications, poses fundamental challenges to classical communication paradigms. In scenarios such as targeted drug delivery, devices operate under severe limitations in energy, size, and communication capabilities, while requiring precise and selective activation within spatially localized regions.
  In this work, we propose the framework of Joint Detection and Identification (JDAI) as a system-level approach for scalable control under such constraints. The key idea is to shift from reliable message transmission to a control-oriented paradigm, in which devices locally decide whether a broadcast signal is relevant. This enables implicit addressing and subset activation without the need for explicit per-device communication.
  We demonstrate how message identification can be combined with sensing. This enables the realization of a closed-loop system that integrates detection, communication, and actuation. Using the example of targeted nanorobot therapy, we analyze the interplay between sensing resolution, communication constraints, and system dynamics. In particular, we show that while identification exhibits favorable asymptotic scaling, practical implementations are governed by finite blocklength effects, noise, and latency.
  The proposed framework complements existing physical-layer communication approaches, including molecular, electromagnetic, and acoustic techniques, by providing a control-layer abstraction for scalable subset selection. Overall, JDAI connects identification-theoretic principles with system-level design to control large, resource-limited environments.

</details>


### [171] [Learning Where to Look: UCB-Driven Controlled Sensing for Quickest Change Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28563)
*Yu-Han Huang,Argyrios Gerogiannis,Subhonmesh Bose,Venugopal V. Veeravalli*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文研究了带匪类反馈和可控感知的多通道最快变点检测问题，提出了两种基于UCB的检测算法，在控制误报的同时实现了渐进最优的检测延迟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在序列数据分析中，快速准确地检测分布变化至关重要。现有方法通常忽略感知资源的优化分配，本文旨在开发能自适应集中感知资源于最信息丰富的流，同时保证误报控制的高效检测算法。

Method: 提出了两种基于UCB多臂匪类算法的检测程序，适应性地选择最信息丰富的数据流进行观测。第一种方法假设已知变化前后的分布，第二种扩展至未知分布（仅知至少一个通道在变化点存在均值偏移）的场景。

Result: 理论分析表明两种方法在标准误报约束下都能实现一阶渐进最优的检测延迟。模拟实验显示其在合成基准测试中始终优于现有方法，并显著减少了计算开销。

Conclusion: 基于UCB的可控感知方法为多通道变点检测提供了高效解决方案，既能保证误报控制，又能实现渐进最优性能，特别适用于非平稳环境中的学习问题。所有方法都具有计算高效的特点。

Abstract: We study the multichannel quickest change detection problem with bandit feedback and controlled sensing, in which an agent sequentially selects one of the data streams to observe at each time-step and aims to detect an unknown change as quickly as possible while controlling false alarms. Assuming known pre- and post-change distributions and allowing an arbitrary subset of streams to be affected by the change, we propose two novel and computationally efficient detection procedures inspired by the Upper Confidence Bound (UCB) multi-armed bandit algorithm. Our methods adaptively concentrate sensing on the most informative streams while preserving false-alarm guarantees. We show that both procedures achieve first-order asymptotic optimality in detection delay under standard false-alarm constraints. We also extend the UCB-driven controlled sensing approach to the setting where the pre- and post-change distributions are unknown, except for a mean-shift in at least one of the channels at the change-point. This setting is particularly relevant to the problem of learning in piecewise stationary environments. Finally, extensive simulations on synthetic benchmarks show that our methods consistently outperform existing state-of-the-art approaches while offering substantial computational savings.

</details>


### [172] [Version AoI Optimization under Power and General Distortion Constraints in Uplink NOMA](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28631)
*Gangadhar Karevvanavar,Rajshekhar V. Bhat,Nikolaos Pappas*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文研究了M用户上行非正交多址系统中版本信息年龄最小化问题，在平均功率和信息质量约束下，通过联合优化调度、比特分配和功率控制，开发了无需跟踪瞬时VAoI的随机策略，在复杂约束条件下实现了对全局最优VAoI的2倍近似保证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在能量受限的多用户NOMA系统中，存在传输比特数（影响信息质量）与功率消耗之间的根本权衡：传输更多比特提高信息质量但减少传输机会并增加VAoI，反之亦然。需要解决在多址容量约束下用户功率分配耦合导致的指数复杂度问题。

Method: 1) 将加权和VAoI最小化问题建模为凸优化问题；2) 设计VAoI无关的静态随机策略，联合优化调度、比特分配和功率控制；3) 利用拉格朗日对偶分解推导调度概率和功率分配的闭式解；4) 高效确定最优连续干扰消除解码顺序，避免穷举搜索。

Result: 提出的策略获得全局最优平均VAoI的2-近似保证。数值结果表明：在高功率预算下，NOMA可实现接近零的VAoI，而TDMA会饱和在非零值；通用失真框架通过为更新中的不同比特分配不等重要性，适应多样的比特优先级结构。

Conclusion: NOMA在VAoI最小化方面显著优于TDMA，特别是在高功率区域。所提出的随机调度策略在保持低复杂度的同时，实现了接近最优的性能，为解决多用户NOMA系统中的信息新鲜度优化问题提供了有效方案。

Abstract: The Version Age of Information (VAoI) quantifies information freshness by measuring the number of versions the receiver lags behind. This paper studies VAoI minimization in an $M$-user uplink non-orthogonal multiple access (NOMA) system where users maintain single-packet buffers and transmissions are constrained by average power and information-quality constraints, modeled by a general distortion function. A fundamental trade-off arises: transmitting more bits per update improves information quality but increases power consumption, reducing transmission opportunities and increasing VAoI, while transmitting fewer bits has the opposite effect. We formulate a weighted-sum VAoI minimization problem as a convex optimization problem. However, users' power allocations are coupled through multiple-access capacity constraints per channel state, leading to exponential complexity. To address this, we develop a VAoI-agnostic stationary randomized policy that jointly optimizes scheduling, bit allocation, and power control without tracking instantaneous VAoI, and achieves a provable 2-approximation to the globally optimal average VAoI. Leveraging Lagrangian dual decomposition, we derive closed-form expressions for the scheduling probabilities and power allocations, and efficiently determine the optimal successive interference cancellation decoding order, avoiding exhaustive search Numerical results show that NOMA significantly outperforms time-division multiple access (TDMA): at high power budgets, NOMA achieves near-zero VAoI, whereas TDMA saturates at a non-zero value, consistent with the analysis. The proposed general distortion framework accommodates diverse bit-priority structures by assigning unequal importance to different bits within an update.

</details>
